Bitcoin Halving is an automatic reduction in profits from an activity called mining, so for each block mined in the network, miners receive half the reward for the same period of time. for mining that block. A block on the Bitcoin blockchain network is a file that stores 1 MB worth of Bitcoin transactions. Mining and halving occur not only for Bitcoin but also for many other coins, such as Litecoin, Zcash, and BitcoinCash.\n\nThe halving process is an important element in the Bitcoin ecosystem and is a powerful mechanism whose practical application allows you to achieve several important goals in maintaining stable and unfavorable operations. disruption of the Bitcoin blockchain.\n\nThe main goal of halving is to limit the rate of cryptocurrency inflation by proportionally reducing the issuance of new coins. The algorithms of cryptocurrencies like Bitcoin do not allow you to print an infinite amount of money. Bitcoin supply is limited to 21,000,000 coins. Due to the halving mechanism in the Bitcoin network, the supply of coins is gradually increasing and is significantly lower than the growth rate of demand for them. Every time a halving occurs, the rate of new coin issuance decreases, helping to balance the growth of the currency supply and prevent unlimited inflation.\n\nBitcoin halving directly affects the change in its value per unit of time. Each halving reduces the flow of new coins into circulation, increasing the price of Bitcoin \u2014 supply decreases while demand continues to increase. This phenomenon is an economic law that operates not only in the cryptocurrency market but also applies to other financial markets and trading instruments. The price of bitcoin is expected to increase exponentially, with each halving as mining reaches the maximum number of coins that can be mined online.\n\nBitcoin halving also enhances the decentralization of the digital asset blockchain because after each reduction in the number of rewards for a block mined in the network, miners have to work harder and more efficiently. more effectively to be able to receive the same amount of block rewards as before. As the cryptocurrency mining industry, especially Bitcoin, grows at a very fast pace, halving can also help increase the number of miners, which increases the security and reliability of the entire network.\n\nIn May 2020, 6.25 bitcoins were allocated per new block. The rate of inflation will halve to 3,125 bitcoins around May 2024 and continue to halve every four years until a total of 21 million Bitcoins are issued in 2140.\n\nTHEO B\u1ea0N GI\u00c1 #Bitcoin So my message to X/Twitter is 'you must comply, we will watch what you do'.\u201d\n\n\u201cX (Twitter) is the platform with the largest proportion of false information, followed by Facebook,\u201d she told reporters.\n\nLarge technology corporations massively removed fake news\n\nThe 200-page EU report presents the work that major platforms have done in the first 6 months of 2023, to prepare for supervision when the new law takes effect from August 25.\n\nAccordingly, LinkedIn's owner, Microsoft, has stopped 6.7 million fake accounts and deleted 24,000 fake news.\n\nYouTube, owned by Google, reported to the EU that it had removed more than \u201c400 channels involved in influence operations linked to the Russian state-sponsored Internet Research Agency.\u201d\n\nTikTok also removed nearly 6 million fake accounts and 410 unverifiable ads.\n\nGoogle removed ads from nearly 300 websites linked to \u201cstate-sponsored propaganda sites\u201d and rejected more than 140,000 political advertisers for \u201cfailing identity verification.\u201d\n\nMeanwhile Meta expanded its fact-checking operations to 26 partners covering 22 languages in the EU, now including Czech and Slovak.\n\nThe report said 37% of users also unshared when informed about fake news. M\u1ed9t trong Thi\u00ean Canh 36 bi\u1ebfn : C\u1ea3i T\u1eed Ho\u00e0n Sinh.\n\nN\u00f3i v\u1ec1 thu\u1eadt n\u00e0y, c\u00f3 t\u00e0i li\u1ec7u ghi ch\u00e9p: \"C\u1ea3i T\u1eed Ho\u00e0n Sinh r\u1ea5t huy\u1ec1n di\u1ec7u, b\u1ecb li\u1ec7t v\u00e0o h\u00e0ng c\u1ea5m thu\u1eadt b\u1edfi v\u00ec c\u00f4ng d\u1ee5ng c\u1ee7a n\u00f3 l\u00e0 c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 \u0111o\u1ea1t l\u1ea1i linh h\u1ed3n ng\u01b0\u1eddi ch\u1ebft t\u1eeb trong d\u00f2ng Lu\u00e2n H\u1ed3i. \u0110\u00f3 l\u00e0 m\u1ed9t h\u00e0nh \u0111\u1ed9ng \u0111i ng\u01b0\u1ee3c l\u1ea1i Thi\u00ean \u0111\u1ea1o v\u00e0 ng\u01b0\u1eddi s\u1eed d\u1ee5ng s\u1ebd ph\u1ea3i hao t\u1ed5n r\u1ea5t nhi\u1ec1u tu vi v\u00e0 ph\u00fac b\u00e1o c\u1ee7a ch\u00ednh m\u00ecnh.\u00a0Tu vi s\u1ebd \u1ea3nh h\u01b0\u1edfng \u0111\u1ebfn ph\u00e1p l\u1ef1c v\u00e0 tu\u1ed5i th\u1ecd, \u0111\u1ed1i v\u1edbi sinh m\u1ec7nh tr\u01b0\u1eddng th\u1ecd nh\u01b0 th\u1ea7n ti\u00ean, vi\u1ec7c m\u1ea5t \u0111i v\u00e0i ng\u00e0n n\u0103m c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 kh\u00f4ng g\u00e2y qu\u00e1 nhi\u1ec1u \u1ea3nh h\u01b0\u1edfng. Nh\u01b0ng m\u1ea5t \u0111i ph\u00fac b\u00e1o th\u00ec l\u1ea1i kh\u00e1c. Ph\u00fac b\u00e1o c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 v\u00ed nh\u01b0 l\u00e0 s\u1ef1 nghi\u1ec7p c\u1ee7a m\u1ed9t v\u1ecb th\u1ea7n ti\u00ean, m\u1ea5t \u0111i ph\u00fac b\u00e1o s\u1ebd \u1ea3nh h\u01b0\u1edfng l\u1edbn \u0111\u1ebfn \u0111\u1ecba v\u1ecb trong t\u01b0\u01a1ng lai c\u1ee7a h\u1ecd\".\n- V\u0169 kh\u00ed l\u00e0 C\u1eedu x\u1ec9 \u0111inh b\u00e0 \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c Th\u00e1i th\u01b0\u1ee3ng l\u00e3o qu\u00e2n \u0111\u00edch th\u00e2n luy\u1ec7n ch\u1ebf.\n\nC\u00f3 m\u1ed9t lu\u1eadn \u0111i\u1ec3m \u0111\u01b0a ra ch\u00ednh l\u00e0: Tr\u01b0 B\u00e1t Gi\u1edbi \u0111\u00e3 s\u1eed d\u1ee5ng c\u1ea5m thu\u1eadt \u0111\u1ec3 c\u1ee9u s\u01b0 huynh c\u1ee7a m\u00ecnh (1).\n\nNgo\u00e0i ra n\u1ebfu n\u00f3i T\u00f4n Ng\u1ed9 Kh\u00f4ng \u0111\u1ea1i n\u00e1o thi\u00ean cung l\u00e0 m\u1ed9t tr\u1eadn m\u01b0a. Th\u00ec tr\u01b0\u1edbc \u0111\u00f3 c\u00f3 2 k\u1ebb \u0111\u00e3 \u0111\u1ea1i n\u00e1o thi\u00ean cung khi\u1ebfn Thi\u00ean \u0110\u00ecnh su\u00fdt b\u1ecb di\u1ec7t vong \u0111\u00f3 l\u00e0 Nh\u1ecb Lang Th\u1ea7n v\u00e0 Thi\u00ean B\u1ed3ng Nguy\u00ean So\u00e1i (2).\n\n(1), (2): Tr\u01b0 B\u00e1t Gi\u1edbi nguy\u00ean l\u00e0 Thi\u00ean B\u1ed3ng Nguy\u00ean So\u00e1i ch\u1ec9 huy h\u01a1n 8 v\u1ea1n thu\u1ef7 binh \u1edf thi\u00ean \u0111\u00ecnh, \u00f4ng tu luy\u1ec7n th\u00e0nh th\u1ea1o 36 ph\u00e9p Thi\u00ean cang c\u1ee7a \u0110\u1ea1o gi\u00e1o. Trong \u0111\u00f3 n\u1ed5i ti\u1ebfng v\u1edbi ph\u00e9p c\u1ea3i t\u1eed ho\u00e0n sinh.\n\nT\u1ea1i tr\u1eadn chi\u1ebfn gi\u1eefa T\u00f4n Ng\u1ed9 Kh\u00f4ng v\u00e0 H\u1ed3ng H\u00e0i Nhi, M\u1eb7c k\u1ec7 s\u1ef1 can ngan c\u1ee7a l\u00e3o Tr\u01b0. T\u00f4n Ng\u1ed9 Kh\u00f4ng b\u1ecb l\u1eeda Tam mu\u1ed9i l\u00e0m m\u00ea man b\u1ea5t t\u1ec9nh, ch\u00ednh Tr\u01b0 B\u00e1t Gi\u1edbi l\u00e0 ng\u01b0\u1eddi c\u1ee9u s\u1ed1ng b\u1edfi trong 36 ph\u00e9p Thi\u00ean Cang c\u00f3 thu\u1eadt c\u1ee9u s\u1ed1ng ng\u01b0\u1eddi, \u0111\u00f3 l\u00e0 thu\u1eadt Kh\u1edfi t\u1eed h\u1ed3i sinh (c\u1ee9u s\u1ed1ng nh\u1eefng ng\u01b0\u1eddi \u0111ang c\u1eadn k\u1ec1 c\u00e1i ch\u1ebft ho\u1eb7c v\u1eeba m\u1edbi ch\u1ebft). N\u1ebfu c\u00f3 thu\u1eadt n\u00e0y trong tay th\u00ec ng\u01b0\u1eddi \u0111\u00f3 nh\u1ea5t \u0111\u1ecbnh r\u1ea5t m\u1ea1nh trong c\u1eedu gi\u1edbi.\n\nNgo\u00e0i ra Tr\u01b0 B\u00e1t Gi\u1edbi c\u00f2n s\u1edf h\u1eefu m\u1ed9t s\u1ed1 ph\u00e9p thu\u1eadt kh\u00e1 \"b\u00e1 \u0111\u1ea1o\" l\u00e0m \u0111i\u00ean \u0111\u1ea3o tr\u1eddi \u0111\u1ea5t nh\u01b0 O\u00e1t to\u00e0n t\u1ea1o h\u00f3a: \u0110i\u1ec1u khi\u1ec3n tr\u1eddi \u0111\u1ea5t, t\u1ea1o ra m\u1ed9t th\u1ebf gi\u1edbi gi\u1ea3 m\u00e0 th\u1eadt, ch\u1ec9 nh\u1eefng ng\u01b0\u1eddi c\u00f3 ph\u00e1p thu\u1eadt cao si\u00eau m\u1edbi luy\u1ec7n \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c chi\u00eau n\u00e0y; \u0110i\u00ean \u0111\u1ea3o \u00e2m d\u01b0\u01a1ng: \u0110\u1ea3o l\u1ed9n \u0111\u1ea5t tr\u1eddi, thay \u0111\u1ed5i nh\u1eefng l\u1ebd th\u01b0\u1eddng c\u1ee7a t\u1ef1 nhi\u00ean, khi\u1ebfn cho v\u1ea1n v\u1eadt di chuy\u1ec3n ng\u01b0\u1ee3c l\u1ea1i v\u1edbi t\u1ea1o h\u00f3a v\u00e0 th\u1ec3 hi\u1ec7n ph\u00e1p l\u1ef1c cao th\u00e2m c\u1ee7a c\u00e1c \u0111\u1ea1o gia; Di tinh ho\u00e1n \u0111\u1ea9u: C\u00f3 th\u1ec3 ho\u00e1n \u0111\u1ed5i v\u1ea1n v\u1eadt trong v\u0169 tr\u1ee5 cho nhau, t\u1eeb Th\u1ea7n th\u00e1nh, con ng\u01b0\u1eddi cho \u0111\u1ebfn c\u00e1c lo\u00e0i th\u00fa v\u1eadt hay qu\u1ef7 qu\u00e1i, y\u00eau ma.\n\nN\u00f3i th\u00eam v\u1ec1 Thi\u00ean B\u1ed3ng Nguy\u00ean So\u00e1i, y \u0111\u00e3 g\u00e2y r\u1eafc r\u1ed1i tr\u00ean thi\u00ean cung kho\u1ea3ng 360 n\u0103m sau khi T\u00f4n Ng\u1ed9 Kh\u00f4ng b\u1ecb \u0111\u00e8 d\u01b0\u1edbi n\u00fai Ng\u0169 H\u00e0nh S\u01a1n. D\u01b0\u1edbi d\u01b0\u01a1ng gian, 360 n\u0103m d\u00e0i \u0111\u1eb1ng \u0111\u1eb5ng tr\u00f4i qua nh\u01b0ng \u0111\u1ed5i l\u1ea1i tr\u00ean thi\u00ean cung m\u1edbi ch\u1ec9 l\u00e0 1 n\u0103m, v\u1eeba hay l\u1ea1i \u0111\u1ebfn d\u1ecbp V\u01b0\u01a1ng M\u1eabu m\u1edf Ti\u1ec7c B\u00e0n \u0110\u00e0o.
